## Diagram 2

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    A[Start Test] --> B{Test Type}
    B -->|test_validate_post| C[Create Valid TripLeg]
    C --> D[Set All Required Fields]
    D --> E[Call validate POST]
    E --> F[Success - No Exception]
    B -->|test_validate_post_with_not_null_id| G[Create TripLeg with ID]
    G --> H[Set Required Fields]
    H --> I[Call validate POST]
    I --> J{ValidationError Raised?}
    J -->|Yes| K[Check Error Message]
    K --> L[Assert: Cannot set uuid]
    B -->|test_validate_post_with_missing_fields| M[Create Empty TripLeg]
    M --> N[Validate Missing All Fields]
    N --> O[Add Fields Incrementally]
    O --> P[Validate After Each Addition]
    P --> Q{More Fields to Add?}
    Q -->|Yes| O
    Q -->|No| R[Validate Type Field]
    R --> S[Set Valid Type]
    S --> T[Test creator_shipment_id vs shipment_number]
    T --> U[Success]
    F --> V[End Test]
    L --> V
    U --> V
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Test as PostTripLegValidatorTest
    participant TripLeg as TripLeg
    participant Validator as TripLegValidator
    participant Error as ValidationError
    Test->>Test: __init__()
    Test->>Validator: Create instance
    Test->>TripLeg: Create new TripLeg()
    Test->>TripLeg: Set solution_id
    Test->>TripLeg: Set owner_organization_fv_id
    Test->>TripLeg: Set carrier_organization_fv_id
    Test->>TripLeg: Set destination_location_code
    Test->>TripLeg: Set origin_location_code
    Test->>TripLeg: Set shipment_number
    Test->>TripLeg: Set creator_shipment_id
    Test->>TripLeg: Set sequence_number
    Test->>TripLeg: Set type
    Test->>Validator: validate(trip_leg, "POST")
    Validator-->>Test: Success
    Test->>TripLeg: Create TripLeg(id="uuid")
    Test->>Validator: validate(trip_leg, "POST")
    Validator->>Error: Raise ValidationError
    Error-->>Test: "Cannot set uuid when creating an object"
    Test->>TripLeg: Create empty TripLeg()
    Test->>Validator: validate(trip_leg, "POST")
    Validator->>Error: Raise ValidationError
    Error-->>Test: "Missing required fields: ..."
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> EmptyTripLeg
    EmptyTripLeg --> SolutionIdSet: Set solution_id
    SolutionIdSet --> OwnerOrgSet: Set owner_organization_fv_id
    OwnerOrgSet --> CarrierOrgSet: Set carrier_organization_fv_id
    CarrierOrgSet --> DestinationSet: Set destination_location_code
    DestinationSet --> OriginSet: Set origin_location_code
    OriginSet --> ShipmentIdSet: Set creator_shipment_id or shipment_number
    ShipmentIdSet --> SequenceSet: Set sequence_number
    SequenceSet --> TypeSet: Set type to PLANNED or ACTUAL
    TypeSet --> ValidTripLeg: All Required Fields Present
    ValidTripLeg --> [*]: Validation Passes
    EmptyTripLeg --> ValidationError: Missing Fields
    SolutionIdSet --> ValidationError: Missing Fields
    OwnerOrgSet --> ValidationError: Missing Fields
    CarrierOrgSet --> ValidationError: Missing Fields
    DestinationSet --> ValidationError: Missing Fields
    OriginSet --> ValidationError: Missing Fields
    ShipmentIdSet --> ValidationError: Missing Fields
    SequenceSet --> ValidationError: Invalid Type
    ValidationError --> [*]: Test Assertion
```
